Military Value in Question, America Abandoning Airship Policy

Many in the Navy Hold This View

Cause of Macon Disaster to be Thoroughly Investigated

[Washington] Due to the Macon's crash, the plan to continue building airships in the United States has obviously been indefinitely shelved. Senior naval officers have declared that the Navy has now ended the airship experiments. This statement has almost received unanimous support from Washington officials. President Roosevelt has declared that he has no intention of asking Congress to allocate funds to build airships to replace the Macon. The President continued, saying that if there were funds, he would prefer to use them to build fifty long-range reconnaissance aircraft rather than another large airship. However, what is now clear is that the President's attitude cannot be regarded as the United States abandoning the airship policy altogether. Although the Civil Aeronautics Committee has suggested building more large airships for transoceanic mail delivery, naval officers have apparently abandoned the airship policy, and most members of Congress also think this way. Representative Vincent, Chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee, declared that he did not want to propose a resolution to build two large airships before Congress investigated the circumstances of the Macon disaster. The Macon's crash has proven that large airships have lost their effectiveness in naval defense. The successive crashes of the Akron and the Macon have made the actual effectiveness of airships a great question. However, Senator Robinson expressed a special opinion, saying that although three airships have crashed and more than a dozen people have died, I believe that the construction of large airships should continue. I think the success of Captain Eckener in piloting the Zeppelin is noteworthy. (National Telegraph on the 14th)

[Washington] Washington announced today, after hearing the news of the crash of the Navy airship Macon, that it would conduct an investigation in two phases to determine the cause of the Macon's crash. The location of the incident was about ten miles off the coast of California. It occurred at night, and a total of two people died. It is said that Chief of Naval Operations Swanson will lead the Navy Department in the first investigation. After the first investigation is completed, it will be followed by a congressional investigation. Government leaders said that some members of Congress may be sent to the Pacific coast to investigate the cause of the Macon disaster. Swanson said that he would organize a naval board of inquiry within two or three days. Mr. Swanson held a long meeting today with Representative Vincent, Chairman of the House Naval Affairs Committee, to discuss the Macon disaster. Mr. Swanson replied to the question of the Navy's last large airship, saying that the Navy Department has not yet made a decision about the future of large airships. Frankly speaking, I really don't know if it is worth building large airships. But the Navy now has more urgent needs. Admiral Reeves, commander of the U.S. Fleet, issued a statement saying that the eighty-one survivors would be on a warship off the coast of San Francisco to recount the Macon disaster. According to naval regulations, the naval court should be composed of three naval officers and one neutral person. To date, statements issued by naval and government officials have unanimously praised the airship's captain, Wiley. (National Telegraph on the 14th)

Amsterdam. Puxin, manager of the Dutch airline, told reporters that although the Macon had crashed, the company still believes that airships are a useful means of transportation. Mr. Ji expressed sympathy for the views of Mr. Eckener, who declared that these unfortunate encounters were all caused by climate change. For example, although the German airship Zeppelin had encountered storms repeatedly, it was still safe and sound. Therefore, the Macon's crash should be investigated, so the Dutch company must also investigate it for reference. (National Telegraph on the 14th)

Captain Recounts the Circumstances of the Disaster

[San Francisco] Wiley, commander of the airship "Macon," explained the cause of the disaster. It is said that the metal structure inside the balloon broke, and the small balloons inside the bag burst. The balloon's crack was blown by the wind and expanded rapidly, so a wireless telegram was sent for help. Later, Wiley ordered the abandonment of the airship. The process was well-ordered. The crew members jumped into the sea one by one and were rescued by lifeboats. Only two people, the wireless operator and the waiter, died because they jumped from forty meters above the water and suffered severe shocks. When the ship touched the surface of the sea, some crew members were still launching rockets at the front of the airship to guide rescue ships. When the airship touched the surface of the sea, the descent speed reached 100 meters per minute. (Havas Radio on the 13th)

Two Missing, the Rest Survived

[San Francisco] The crash of the U.S. Navy airship Macon yesterday will cause the U.S. Navy authorities to no longer build lighter-than-air airships. It is expected that the Navy Department and Congress will begin investigating the cause of the crash within a few days. The Macon sank about one hundred and ten miles southwest of San Francisco at a depth of 250 fathoms. It is said that the authorities do not intend to salvage it. Two crew members died. The rest were transported here by warship today. When the Macon was flying back to Sunnyvale base, it encountered bad weather and heavy fog. Suddenly, one of the twelve gas chambers in the ship exploded, so the ship's bow faced the sky and the stern faced the ground, gradually descending from a height of 1,250 feet. Although the crew members wanted to make it parallel, it was ineffective. After the ship touched the water, the crew members escaped in rubber lifeboats and were later rescued by a warship. As for the two missing people, they have probably drowned, and their bodies have not yet been found. (Reuters on the 13th)

Britain Will Propose Expanding the Scope of the Sky Convention at the Naval Conference

China, Japan, the United States, and Russia Are All Among Those Invited

Protect Civilians from Bombing During Wartime

[London] Officials here indicated today that when the Ottawa naval conference is reopened, it may be proposed that the world's major powers conclude a convention to protect each other in the event of war. The countries invited to the convention will probably include Britain, the United States, China, Japan, and Russia. The content of the proposal is not detailed, but it is said to be roughly the same as the recently established Anglo-French agreement. The contracting countries will jointly prevent aerial attacks. The purpose of this agreement is to protect women, children, and innocent people from the dangers of aerial attacks. The Anglo-French agreement has been valued by the world's political circles, because the conditions of the Treaty of Versailles that prohibited Germany from reorganizing its military have been abolished by this agreement. The United States has not yet been invited to participate, probably because the American people do not like this kind of combination. However, European coordination is also highly valued by the American people, so if all countries in the world agree to protect each other, the United States may also be able to participate. (National Telegraph on the 13th)

Lindbergh Kidnapping Case: Hauptmann Sentenced to Death

To be Executed Within a Week After March 18th

Defense Attorney to File Appeal

Flemington – Bruno Hauptmann, the perpetrator in the Lindbergh baby kidnapping case, was sentenced to death by a jury today and will be executed on March 18th. The jury foreman, Mr. Watson, read the verdict stating that Hauptmann was guilty. Hauptmann stood still with a smile. The defense attorney, Mr. Reilly, was furious upon hearing the verdict and declared that he would appeal to the Supreme Court. The jury deliberated for eleven hours and twenty minutes before delivering the verdict at 10:44 PM. Lindbergh was not present in court. Prior to the announcement, military police cleared the courtroom of onlookers before bringing Hauptmann in. The jury, including four women, appeared pale and mentally exhausted when they retired at 10:35 PM. Hauptmann's wife was also in the audience. After the verdict, Hauptmann seemed confident of acquittal. Three days ago, he even told the press that he had won. Officials believe the guilty verdict is a major victory in the government's two-year campaign to eradicate kidnappers. Evidence against Hauptmann was collected through the collaboration of federal and state governments, making it no easy feat. Thus, even though Hauptmann claimed that the ransom money was given to him by his deceased friend, Mr. Fisch, he could not escape the law. Colonel Lindbergh's son was kidnapped on March 1, 1932, and murdered the same night. His body was found seventy-two days later, by which time Lindbergh had paid a ransom of $50,000. For two years, the government has been investigating the case until Hauptmann was arrested for attempting to use gold certificates that had been withdrawn from circulation. (National Telegram, 13th)

Flemington - Bruno Hauptmann, the suspect in the kidnapping of Colonel Lindbergh's young son, has been sentenced to death by a jury. After the foreman read the verdict, Judge Trenchard asked each of the other eleven jurors, one by one, in the same words, to which each juror replied in the same words, "The defendant is indeed guilty of first-degree murder." The courtroom was silent and filled with a deathly atmosphere. Each time a juror answered, Hauptmann would slightly shake his head and look at his wife, but his composure did not change. Judge Trenchard then decided that the execution would take place within a week after March 18th. If Hauptmann wishes to appeal, he has only three avenues: first, the New Jersey Supreme Court, and if rejected, then the Court of Errors and Appeals, and finally, the Court of Pardons, presided over by the Governor of New Jersey, as only the Court of Pardons has the power to commute a death sentence to life imprisonment, or to release a person serving a life sentence early. All these appellate bodies cannot begin to hear the case before May due to procedural reasons. Also, according to custom, prisoners sentenced to death are absolutely forbidden from speaking in prison, but this time Judge Trenchard has specifically allowed Hauptmann to talk to the jailers. The defense attorney, Mr. Reilly, is preparing an appeal, and believes that the prosecution presented by Judge Trenchard to the jury was biased and unfair, and will present thirty-two reasons to support the appeal. (Havas Telegram, 14th)

Flemington – After the court sentenced Bruno Hauptmann, the kidnapper of Colonel Lindbergh's son, to death, he has little hope left. This is because Judge Trenchard of this court is a highly respected legal elder of seventy-two years, and no case that he has judged has ever had the original verdict overturned on appeal. Furthermore, according to the speculation of Hauptmann's defense attorney, Hauptmann is penniless and it will be difficult to pursue an appeal. (Havas Telegram, 14th)

Wealthy Enemies Framed My Son

Heartfelt Words from a Seventy-Year-Old Mother

[Berlin] Hauptmann's mother, who is seventy years old and lives in Kamenz, Saxony, Germany, almost fainted today when she heard that her son had been sentenced to death. Later, with a sobbing voice, she told a Reuters reporter, "My son did not commit this brutal crime. The American authorities fabricated evidence and framed him. He is a poor child who is hated by the rich. How could he win? Now, the only hope lies in Attorney Reilly, who will file an appeal." (Reuters Telegram, 14th)

Death of Renowned British Sinologist Herbert Giles

[London] Herbert Giles, formerly the British Vice-Consul in Shanghai, passed away today at the age of ninety. He joined the British Consulate in China in 1867 and served as Vice-Consul in Shanghai, Ningbo, and other places from 1880. He retired in 1893. From 1897 to 1932, he was a lecturer in Chinese at Cambridge University and a renowned Sinologist. He authored many books on Chinese literature, life, and language. (Reuters Telegram, 13th)

British Mediation Eases Tensions Between Italy and Abyssinia

Establishment of a Demilitarized Border Zone

Negotiations Between the Two Countries Have Not Reached an Understanding

[Rome] The clouds of war between Italy and Abyssinia seemed to dissipate slightly today. Government officials from both countries met throughout the day, apparently with some results, which eased the serious situation somewhat. After the Italian Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Suvich, met with the Abyssinian Chargé d'Affaires in Italy, Mr. Yessous, Mr. Yessous declared, "Abyssinian troops have not invaded the border of Italian Somaliland. All disturbances are caused by nomadic tribes who are not under the control of the Abyssinian government." Subsequently, Mr. Suvich and Mr. Yessous expressed hope that the events between the two countries could be resolved without bloodshed. At the same time, however, the war preparations of both countries continued. More than 30,000 Italian troops remained on standby in Florence and Milan. Prime Minister Mussolini personally convened the Supreme Defense Council to discuss the Abyssinian issue in detail. On the Abyssinian side, the government announced that it hoped the League of Nations could mediate and avoid war, but it would be difficult to accept the demands to salute the Italian people and pay compensation of 5 million yuan. It is learned that meetings will still be held in the capitals of both countries in an attempt to avoid conflict between the two countries. (National Telegram, 13th)

[Rome] Various countries are now actively engaged in diplomatic negotiations to resolve the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia. The main negotiations are taking place in the Abyssinian capital, with the Abyssinian Prince and the Italian Minister consulting. On the other hand, the Abyssinian Chargé d'Affaires in Italy, Mr. Yessous, met with the Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Suvich, and was received by Prime Minister Mussolini. During the meeting with Mr. Suvich, he stated that the military measures taken by Italy so far were only precautionary. It is generally believed that the resolution of this dispute will likely involve the establishment of a neutral zone at the border between Abyssinia and the Italian East African colonies, and the dispatch of a joint commission by the two countries to determine responsibility for the incident. (Havas Telegram, 13th)

[Rome] The Abyssinian Chargé d'Affaires visited Italian Undersecretary of Foreign Affairs, Mr. Suvich, this afternoon and was received by Mr. Suvich for about an hour. There was no official news release about the content of the talks or the results of the negotiations, but according to sources, there is still no concrete agreement on the possibility of establishing a neutral zone between Italy and Abyssinia to prevent the situation from becoming more complicated. However, Italian political circles have repeatedly stated that the Italian government only wants a peaceful resolution, but it is still a question whether the Abyssinian Emperor has sufficient authority to prohibit his subordinates from looting and killing. (National Telegram, 13th)

Simon Reports to the House of Commons

Both Armies Maintain Original Positions

Direct Negotiations Underway

[London] Foreign Secretary Simon spoke in the House of Commons today about the dispute between Italy and Abyssinia, stating that the British Ambassador to Rome learned that after a conflict occurred in the Somaliland border area, the Italian government mobilized two army divisions, totaling 30,000 troops, in Italy. The British Ambassador also learned that the Italian government's plan was not to abandon direct negotiations with Abyssinia in order to achieve a peaceful resolution. According to recent news, Italian troops have not advanced further from their positions in the disputed area, and the Italian Minister to Abyssinia has been instructed to negotiate with the Abyssinian government. The British government has also instructed the British Minister to Abyssinia, Mr. Barton, to do his best to mediate and ensure the success of these negotiations. Reports that Italy had sent an ultimatum to Abyssinia have been denied by the authorities. However, the Italian government lodged a protest with the Abyssinian government after the recent border incident and reserved the right to seek compensation. As for Abyssinia, it is complying with its January 19th document to the League of Nations and has strictly ordered its frontline troops not to cause further incidents. (Reuters Telegram, 13th)

Germany Drafts Reply to Anglo-French Proposals

To Be Sent to the British and French Governments and Published Simultaneously

[Berlin] People are currently awaiting Germany's reply to the Anglo-French London Declaration of February 3rd. This reply will be sent by the German government to the British and French Ambassadors to Germany this Thursday or Friday, who will then forward it to the British and French governments. The full text of the reply has been drafted and is currently awaiting approval from Prime Minister Hitler. It will probably not be published immediately in Berlin, but will be announced simultaneously after agreement with Britain and France. The tone of the reply is likely to be very moderate, but the wording will be mostly vague and non-committal. The German government intends to avoid two difficulties and therefore has to use ambiguous language. Firstly, the people of other countries are trying to unite to seek peace, and Germany does not want to give the impression of passively not participating. Secondly, because the political situation in various countries is very unstable, Germany wants to avoid being subject to basic constraints, so as to wait for the right moment to act. The German government is paying close attention to the internal political changes in Britain, France, Russia, and other countries. The recent conflict between Italy and Abyssinia has been met with calm by Germany, as if it were unrelated to Germany. In fact, this is a deliberate attempt to conceal the situation from foreign powers, as Italy's colonial conflict inevitably reduces its freedom of action in European politics. Those with discerning eyes know this. In addition, Germany seems to want to misinterpret the London Declaration as a preliminary recognition of Germany's right to rearm, and even if the London Declaration does not immediately recognize Germany's right to rearm, at least the powers will no longer strongly oppose it. Therefore, Germany can take advantage of the opportunity to gain more advantages. The longer the negotiations are delayed, the more Germany's military will expand. Moreover, it is worth noting that the most influential people in Germany have now taken a further step. The most influential members of the Nazi Party, such as Alfred Rosenberg, the director of the Nazi Party's Foreign Affairs Bureau, who is greatly relied upon by Hitler, are now reviving the famous theory of former Vice-Chancellor Papen, advocating that European countries unite to conquer Soviet Russia. It is hoped that this proposition will gain the sympathy of some people in Britain. From this, it can be seen that influential elements in Germany have various plans, and their power is difficult to predict. However, on the eve of the delivery of Germany's reply, we may as well elaborate on it. (Havas Telegram, 14th)

[London] The Labour Party will introduce a motion of impeachment against the government in the House of Commons today, accusing the government of ineffective handling of the unemployment problem. Injection of Liquid Enhances Coal Combustion Power

New Japanese Invention

[Tokyo] Fuel is an important national policy, and it is also the focus of parliamentary debate. This time, Mr. Takeichi Goro, a merchant in Tokyo, has invented a liquid that, when injected into coal, causes the coal powder, which originally had very little heat, to suddenly generate intense combustion with extremely strong heat. It has been successfully tested. If this liquid is used, the value of one ton of coal can be reduced by four yen, which is very economical. Based on the current fuel consumption, it can save 45 million yen per year. The Navy, the Ministry of Railways, various shipping companies, and factories will regard this as a revolution in the fuel industry, which is very noteworthy. (Japanese United Press Telegram, 14th)

Derailment of the Extra Train on the Peiping-Mukden Railway near Peiping

[Tianjin] Extra train number 102 on the Peiping-Mukden Railway departed from Tianjin at 0:10 on the 14th. At around 2:00 AM, when it reached the area between An Ding and Wanzhuang, the locomotive derailed due to the rotting of sleepers and the loosening of spikes. The eleven cars behind the locomotive also derailed, with seven overturning next to the tracks. The extent of the damage to passengers and cargo is still being investigated. By about 4:00 AM, the Tianjin General Bureau of the Peiping-Mukden Railway sent workers on a rescue train to expedite repairs. Traffic was interrupted for half a day and was restored at 2:30 PM. The eastward-bound trains numbers 3, 4, and 43 on the Peiping-Mukden Railway have all been diverted to depart from Tianjin. The express train from Shanhaiguan to Peiping was repaired, and travelled from Tianjin to Peiping. (Special Telegram, 14th)

[Tianjin] The derailment of the 102nd passenger-freight train on the Peiping-Tianjin section of the Peiping-Mukden Railway this morning occurred between Weishanzhuang and An Ding. From the 13th car onwards, all the way to the 33rd car, completely derailed. The damage was very light, and no passengers were injured. Repairs took half a day. Passenger trains numbers 3 and 4 between Peiping and Tianjin were suspended, and the schedules of all other trains were delayed by half an hour to an hour. (Special Telegram, 14th)

[Peiping] This morning, the 102nd train on the Peiping-Mukden Railway was carrying a large quantity of sleepers. As it traveled from Tianjin to Peiping, sleepers fell off and landed across the tracks, causing all eleven freight cars attached to the train to derail, halting both northbound and southbound traffic between Peiping and Tianjin. Traffic was restored at 1:15 PM. The Peiping-Pukou and Peiping-Shanghai trains, which were originally scheduled to arrive in Peiping in the morning, will be delayed until 6:00 or 7:00 PM. (Special Telegram, 14th)

[Peiping] A freight train from Peiping to Tianjin derailed between An Ding and Weishanzhuang this morning. A total of thirteen cars overturned, and approximately 80 meters of tracks and sleepers were damaged. No one was injured. Repairs were completed in the afternoon. (Special Telegram, 14th)

Shooting by Taiwanese Against Police Occurs in Xiamen

The location is in a Taiwanese-operated gambling den.

Dozens of shots fired, injuring one passerby.

Xiamen Correspondence: Tian Songmei, a squad leader of the armed police patrol team of the Xiamen Public Security Bureau, and six others were resting in front of No. 5 Kaiyuan Road (i.e., Fuyu) on the evening of the 9th on their bicycles. Outside the foreign company was a coffee shop, and the upper floor in the back was a gambling den operated by Taiwanese. Not long after the armed police rested, the upper floor suddenly opened fire and shot at them, five shots in a row. Wang Xiuxian, the squad leader of the walking armed police team, immediately led several armed police to rush to the scene upon hearing the news. The upper floor fired several more shots, all aimed at the armed police and the patrol team. The armed police patrol team did not return fire. Upon being informed, the Second Branch immediately dispatched Inspector Zhao Guanghou to lead a special team to stop them. The upper floor continued to fire 60 to 70 shots. Tian Songmei and Wang Xiuxian arrested four people at the Fuxing gambling den: one was Guo Jinsheng from Siming, and three were Su Ben, Su Liu, and Su Mu, all from Haicheng. Later, Jiang Jun, a Taiwanese, was also arrested at the Fuxing gambling den. All were taken to the Second Branch. Guo Jinsheng and the other four claimed that they were drinking tea at the Mingxing Tea House next to the Fuxing gambling den and were mistakenly arrested. Jiang Jun was the accountant of the Fuxing Foreign Company and was arrested when he returned to the Fuxing gambling den after visiting a friend on Chenguang Road. All were sent to the General Bureau. According to a report from the Criminal Investigation Team of the Public Security Bureau, the shooting occurred on the upper floor of the Fuxing Foreign Company at No. 5 Kaiyuan Road at 9:35 PM. The reason was that Jiang Jun and another Taiwanese person inexplicably held handguns and fired into the street in front of the building for fun. Feng Lin, the guard policeman of the Second Branch, and the armed police and patrol team went forward to stop them. The shooters did not listen, but instead said bad words and fired a shot at the armed police before entering the Mingxing Tea House. Then, they rushed out and walked into the Fuxing Foreign Company. At that time, several shots were fired from the second floor of Fuxing, and the third floor also fired in response. For a time, the sound of gunfire was loud, with a total of 60 to 70 shots fired, all aimed at the armed police and the patrol team on the street. The armed police and others also fired several shots into the sky. In front of the Kaiyuan Inn across from Fuxing, a passerby named Li Gu was shot in the foot, and a pool of blood formed. He was helped away by his companions. The armed police and patrol team saw the shooting from the upper floor and, ignoring the opposition, bravely went upstairs and arrested Jiang Jun and five others. At that time, the Japanese Police Substation of the Japanese Consulate also sent people to suppress the situation. The upper floor fired three more shots before stopping. It is said that the reason for the Taiwanese shooting for no reason was that the patrol team was resting in front of Fuxing, and the owner of the gambling den believed that the presence of the police at the door prevented gamblers from entering, which hindered his business, so he shot and threatened them, wanting to urge the police to leave. Later, seeing that the police did not leave, but instead came to stop them, they became angry and fired straight ahead. The Fuyu area is where many tea houses and inns where singing girls gather are located, and it is very lively at night. As a result of the shooting lasting for thirty minutes, passersby were shocked and fled, and shops closed their doors, causing great chaos. Afterwards, the Taiwanese side claimed that electric sparklers were set off upstairs, and the armed police fired shots and destroyed the Fuxing gambling den, instigating the Japanese consulate to lodge a negotiation. However, as of the 10th, the Japanese consul had only taken back Jiang Jun, the Taiwanese person, and there was no other movement. (February 13)

Songjiang

The Anti-Smoking Committee Thoroughly Investigates Unlicensed Smoking

The First Branch of the Tinglin Public Security Bureau recently arrested six people, including Wang Helin, for unlicensed smoking and transferred them to the County Anti-Smoking Committee for interrogation. Wang Helin and others stated that they smoked at the Fuji smoking sales shop in Hougang, believing that Yang Ruifu, the manager of the sales shop, had violated the regulations. The Bureau was ordered to summon Yang Ruifu to the case. Yesterday, Yao Naiqian, the secretary of the County Anti-Smoking Committee, held a hearing and interrogated him. However, Yang Ruifu flatly denied that he had been framed by Wang Helin and others, claiming that he had always complied with the regulations and did not sell to unlicensed smokers, and asked for an investigation. Secretary Yao then ruled that since both sides had their own stories, there was suspicion, and ordered that the case be transferred to the County Government for investigation.

Wuxi

Police Officer Assaults Firefighters

The situation escalates, the whole city goes on strike

The Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau of this city and the Beiyi Fire Brigade in Butang Lane had a conflict due to a false fire alarm caused by catching gamblers. The Beiyi Fire Brigade, the Ninth Branch of the Merchant Corps, and the Da'anzhen Township Office were all destroyed, and the miscellaneous items in the Fifth Branch were also damaged by idlers, resulting in a strike. The twelve fire engines, both motorized and hand-operated, were hired by the Firefighting Federation to be dragged to the brigade and parked inside, awaiting mediation by party and government agencies. This has already been noted in this newspaper. It is now learned that County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, in order to resolve the dispute as soon as possible, in addition to ordering all the police officers of the Fifth Branch to return to their posts, also donated 100 yuan of his salary to reward the police officers of the Bureau, and Police Chief Chen also rewarded the entire police force with 60 yuan, stipulating that each police chief would be rewarded with 3.5 silver dollars, each police officer with 2 yuan, and each firefighter with 1.5 yuan. Police Chief Chen also summoned all the police officers to give a speech, and the strike came to an end. However, because the fire brigades had not achieved a satisfactory result, they were unwilling to take back the motorized and hand-operated fire engines parked in the Federation. Yesterday (the 14th) at around 2 AM, a fire suddenly broke out at the home of Li Jiazong, a resident of Nancangmen outside the East Gate. The Beishisanduan Fire Brigade immediately sounded the steel gong alarm. However, because the fire brigades had a dispute with the Fifth Branch and had not been resolved, they did not come to the scene to put out the fire. Only the fire dragon of this section pumped water to put out the fire, but it was a drop in the bucket and did not help, causing the fire to spread to the left and right neighbors. For a time, order was disrupted, and the sound of crying was heart-wrenching. It took about an hour of burning before the fire was extinguished. In total, several shops were burned down, including a pancake shop, a dumpling shop, a barbershop, and a tiger stove shop, with dozens of houses and heavy losses. When the fire was raging, some firefighters went to the gate of the Public Security Bureau on Sanhuang Street and rang the gong, suddenly having an argument with the guards at the gate of the Public Security Bureau, followed by a conflict. The situation was tense, and the police officers fired two blank shots as a warning and took five firefighters who were leading the way into custody. Meanwhile, Police Chief Chen ordered all personnel of the Bureau to be on alert, and a temporary curfew was declared within fifty or sixty steps of the Public Security Bureau. The area under Hongni Bridge was maintained by plainclothes detectives of the Criminal Investigation Team, Chief Wu of Political Affairs Police, and Chief Zhong of Criminal Investigation. Members of the fire brigades from various sections heard that the firefighters had been detained and rushed to ring the gong everywhere, gathering hundreds of people and heading to the Public Security Bureau to demand their release. The Firefighting Federation learned of this and sent staff member Gu Hesheng to the General Bureau to meet with Police Chief Chen and Inspector Wang, where both sides stated what had happened. The detainees were Zhou Fuquan of Beiyi, Sun Meigen of Beisan, Dong Jingen of Beiliu, Wang Anan of Beishier, and Wang Awu of Beishisan. They were handed over to Mr. Gu to be released. However, Wang Awu, Sun Meigen, and others were beaten on their right legs, heads, backs, right chests, etc., with the butts of guns, and were sent to the Brothers Hospital for treatment. Their injuries were serious and their lives were in danger. The merchants of this city, because the fire brigades did not put out the fire, had lost their protection, so starting at 8 AM, all the shops in the city went on strike, and the strike was difficult to resolve. The city was in a state of panic. At 11 AM, Yang Hanxi, Qian Sunqing, Cai Rongsan, Chen Zhanru, Cheng Jingtang, Zhang Fulin, Zhao Zixin, Qian Zhongliang, etc., from the Joint Chamber of Commerce paid a visit to County Magistrate Yan to discuss a solution, explaining that the firefighters had three requests: (1) Wu Zhengrong, Chief of Political Affairs Police of the County Government, would send the twelve fire engines parked at the Firefighting Federation back to the respective fire brigades with red silk. (2) The losses of the Beiyi section and the damaged parts of the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau would be borne by each party, and a resolution would be made later. (3) Chen Yuchu, the County Public Security Bureau Chief, whose handling of affairs was hasty and inappropriate, would be dismissed. If the above three measures could be taken, the strike might not escalate. As a result, County Magistrate Yan expressed acceptance of points one and two, and the third point would be submitted to the province for approval. However, the County Chamber of Commerce must first diligently guide all industries to resume business to avoid losses. Mr. Yang and others agreed to first persuade them to resume business. The injured firefighters Wang Awu and Sun Meigen and six others submitted to the local branch hospital for an examination of their injuries. The Public Security Bureau also telegraphed the province to request instructions on how to handle the situation and deployed the Water Patrol Team to the Bureau for defense. At the same time, Yang Hanxi, Chairman of the Merchant Corps, issued an order to all merchant corps in the county to arm themselves and patrol the streets in this extraordinary period. The County Party Department, the County Chamber of Commerce, and the Firefighting Federation issued an urgent notice, setting a temporary emergency meeting at 2 PM to discuss how to resolve the matter. Cheng Jingtang, Jiang Daoshan, Cai Yourong, Shi Qinglin, Miao Dongchen, Zhang Hanzheng, Gong Haiqin, and sixty or seventy others attended. Zhao Zixin chaired the meeting. First, Cheng Jingtang, Qian Zhongliang, Cai Yourong, and other representatives who went to the County Government reported on their meeting with County Magistrate Yan Shenyu. Then, they discussed the solution. (1) In the case of the Beiyi Fire Brigade and the Fifth Branch of the Public Security Bureau, the Chief of Political Affairs Police Wu Zhengrong would follow the County Magistrate's goodwill and send the fire engines back to the fire brigade. (2) The Chamber of Commerce would work with the Party Department and the Chamber of Commerce to persuade all industries to open for business and maintain local security. (3) The County Public Security Bureau's detention of firefighters without cause would be reported to the County Government for handling with the injured reports of each section. After the discussion, the meeting was adjourned. Police Chief Wu immediately ordered the political police to send the fire dragons to their respective fire brigade temples. Yang Hanxi, Cai Rongsan, Chen Zhanru, Qian Sunqing, and representatives of the County Chamber of Commerce, and Zhao Zixin, Cheng Jingtang, Cai Yourong, Jiang Daoshan, etc., from the Firefighting Federation, set out to persuade the merchants to open for business. Yang Fenglou, a police officer injured by the County Public Security Bureau, submitted to the local branch hospital for an examination of his injuries. After Chief Prosecutor Qian held a court session to examine the injury marks, he ordered them to be sent back. The Beiyi Fire Brigade also filed a criminal lawsuit with the court yesterday regarding the destroyed parts. The County Party Department also convened a temporary emergency talk at around 3 PM, attended by County Magistrate Yan Shenyu and local figures Feng Yunchu, Jiang Daoshan, Qian Sunqing, Shi Qinglin, Qian Zhongliang, and more than a dozen others. Xu Chizi, a member of the Standing Committee of the County Party Department, chaired the meeting. First, the chairman reported the significance of the meeting, stating that the primary issue at present was to persuade all industries to open for business and resume operations, and that the parts concerning injuries and damages would be discussed later. Everyone agreed. The meeting was adjourned. At the same time, the County Party Department telegraphed the Provincial Party Department, requesting that it forward a letter to the Provincial Government, requesting that it send a senior official to Wuxi as soon as possible to impartially mediate the case, so as to avoid further escalation of the strike. The County Party Department also convened the Provincial-Wuxi Teachers College and junior high schools and other schools of boy scouts to form a temporary team to take on defense, patrol, intelligence, and sentry duties to maintain local security. The County Security Brigade Headquarters issued an emergency order, ordering the first, second, and third squadrons to send teams to patrol overnight to prevent accidents. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, the mediation of the case has come to an end, and he immediately used a long-distance telephone to inform the Civil Affairs Department of the Provincial Government and request instructions on how to handle the matter.

Local News

President Wang's Arrival in Shanghai Yesterday

Physical Examination Results Favorable

Meeting with Kong and Soong, Returning to Nanjing Today

Central News Agency reports: President of the Executive Yuan, Wang Jingwei, accompanied by his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, arrived in Shanghai yesterday morning at 7:00 AM on the overnight express train from Nanjing. Mr. Wang's visit is due to a brief respite from government affairs, specifically to undergo a physical examination and to separately visit Wang Fu, Chairman of the Political Reorganization Committee stationed in Peiping; Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance; Soong Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council; Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways; and Chen Shaokuan, Minister of the Navy. He is scheduled to return to Nanjing today. Details of his arrival in Shanghai are recorded as follows:

Arrival in Shanghai Yesterday Morning for Examination of Old Illness

Although President Wang's old illness has been cured, he follows doctor's orders to come to Shanghai every two weeks for a physical examination to prevent recurrence. Yesterday morning, President Wang, accompanied by his wife, Ms. Chen Bijun, and Zeng Zhongming, Vice Minister of Railways, arrived in Shanghai on the overnight express train. After disembarking at Zhenru Station, Mr. Wang and his party immediately transferred to a private car and returned to their private residence to rest. Soon after, he telephoned Dr. Noel, a German doctor, for a physical examination. The results were favorable.

Visiting Huang Fu to Confer on Political Affairs

After completing his physical examination, President Wang, accompanied by Vice Minister of Railways Zeng Zhongming, went to Qiqi Road at about 9:00 AM to visit Huang Fu, Chairman of the Political Reorganization Committee stationed in Peiping, to discuss political affairs and urge Mr. Huang to take office as Minister of Interior in Nanjing as soon as possible. Mr. Huang had been staying in Shanghai for treatment of an arm ailment, but is gradually recovering, so he can take office in Nanjing within a short period. However, the exact date has not yet been decided. As for Mr. Huang's return to the north, the date will be determined after he arrives in Nanjing and assumes his concurrent position as Minister of Interior. Wang and Huang talked for half an hour before Wang left, then went to Noel Hospital at about 11:00 AM for a re-examination and met with Gu Mengyu, Minister of Railways, at the hospital. He did not return to his residence until noon.

Visiting Kong and Soong to Inquire and Confer

President Wang went to West Aihams Road at about 2:00 PM to visit Kong Xiangxi, Minister of Finance, who is ill, and did not leave until about 3:00 PM. He then went to Qiqi Road to visit Soong Ziwen, Standing Committee Member of the National Economic Council. Mr. Soong had also been suffering from a minor illness, so he made a special trip to inquire about his health and to discuss matters related to the future conduct of the National Economic Council's affairs. He did not leave until 3:30 PM, returning to the Zeng residence on Jiao'er Road to rest.

Receiving Wang Chonghui and Many Others

After returning to the Zeng residence, Mr. Wang received Central Committee member Wang Chonghui for discussions. Huang Fu, responding to Mr. Wang's invitation, drove to the residence at 5:45 PM to meet with him. Chen Shaokuan, Minister of the Navy, also came to pay his respects at 6:15 PM. They all had dinner at the Zeng residence, engaging in lively discussions about political affairs. The famous performer Mei Lanfang also visited at about 6:00 PM to discuss matters related to his trip to Russia. He was received by Vice Minister Zeng, who arranged for him to depart with Ambassador Yan on the 18th.

Huang Musong Expected to Arrive in Shanghai This Noon

Central Government Appoints Special Envoy Huang Musong to Tibet to Offer Sacrifices to the Dalai Lama

Huang Musong, the special envoy sent by the central government to offer sacrifices to the Dalai Lama in Tibet, returned to China last winter via India and Nepal. He disembarked in Hong Kong last month and traveled to Guangdong province for a short visit. He left Hong Kong on the Changxing Company's Asia Empress ship the day before yesterday and is returning north, scheduled to arrive in Shanghai at noon today, docking at the Gonghexing Wharf on Broadway Road. Mr. Huang plans to enter Nanjing immediately after arriving in Shanghai to report everything to the central government, it is said.

Sharp Increase in Chinese Goods Exported to the United States Last Year

More Than Eight Million US Dollars More Than the Previous Year

The Great American Evening Post reports: According to statistics on China's exports to the United States in 1934, released today (the 14th) by the US Consulate General, various commodities totaled US$42,410,501, an increase of US$8,168,322 compared to 1933. Inedible animals and animal products ranked first, totaling US$14,454,224. Textiles ranked second, totaling US$11,631,215. Inedible plant products (excluding fibers and wood) ranked third, totaling US$9,096,179. This category saw a significant increase compared to 1933, which was only US$2,614,849. Other categories saw varying increases and decreases. China shipped 50,727,561 ounces of silver to the United States in 1934, a decrease of about 1.2 million ounces compared to 1933, but the value was higher than in 1933. In 1933, it was worth US$16,096,871, while in 1934, it was worth US$22,540,383. Gold shipments to the United States decreased significantly in 1934, with almost no gold bars. In 1933, it was worth US$3,339,739, while in 1934, it was only worth US$171,960.

He also invited US Consul General Cunningham, Judge Hale of the US Assessor's Office, and Yu Hongjun, Secretary-General of the Municipal Government, to accompany him. Sino-European Art Exhibition

To Be Held in Shanghai on the Second of Next Month

Many Works by Famous Hungarian and Austrian Artists

Mr. Galaai, a famous Hungarian artist, arrived in Shanghai last week from Europe, bringing with him many famous works by Hungarian and Austrian art experts from Central Europe, with the intention of holding an exhibition in Shanghai. The exhibition is scheduled to start around the second of next month and last for two weeks. This exhibition includes many works by famous Hungarian, Austrian, and Wu painters, and has been held in major cities in Europe, Syria, Egypt, and India, receiving praise from people everywhere. This is the first time it has been exhibited in China. The person in charge is Galaai, and the sponsors are Ma Yinliang, Zhang Zhuping, Pan Zhiquan, Mei Huaquan, and others. Art lovers will surely feast their eyes at that time, it is said.

Swiss Industrial Exhibition

Consulate in Shanghai Negotiating China's Participation

Central News Agency reports: Switzerland is a region of excellent scenery and a country of exquisite craftsmanship. An industrial exhibition will be held in Basel, Switzerland, on March 30th of this year, welcoming countries from all over the world to visit. The Swiss authorities will provide a warm reception. According to the Central News Agency reporter's inquiries with the Swiss Consulate in Shanghai, the details are as follows:

Industrial Exhibition According to a spokesperson for the Swiss Consulate to the reporter, the industrial exhibition to be held in Basel will feature the most exquisite products from various manufacturers in the country. Switzerland is an industrial country, and its foreign trade is mainly in industrial products, so the progress in craftsmanship is extremely rapid. A total of 21 groups will participate, displaying 1,200 kinds of industrial products, such as various horsepower machines, electrical appliances, instruments, clocks, jewelry, chemicals, medical products, silk fabrics, wool fabrics, embroidered fabrics, boots and shoes, chocolate, sugar chains, milk powder, and cream, all of which are world-renowned products.

Welcome to Visit The Swiss authorities have instructed their consulates in various countries to be responsible for liaising with the host countries regarding visits to the exhibition. Guidance and great convenience will be provided for travel and accommodation after arrival. Switzerland is also a country lacking raw materials, so it especially welcomes raw material countries to visit and exchange goods with Switzerland. It is currently being negotiated by the consulate in Shanghai whether China will send a group to participate at that time, it is said.

Municipal Government Cancels Joint Military-Police Defense

All Restrictions to Be Lifted by the End of This Month

Temporary Martial Law to Be Implemented in Special Circumstances

China Travel Service Declares Completion of Contract for Peiping-Shenyang Through Train

Pilot Operation for Six Months Has Expired, Ministry of Railways Approves Termination

The China Travel Service was entrusted by the Ministry of Railways last July to participate in the organization of the Oriental Travel Agency to handle the Peiping-Shenyang through train service. The contract expired at the end of last year, and the mission was completed. After reporting to the Ministry of Railways for record, the company received an official letter from the ministry yesterday approving the termination. The details are recorded as follows:

Contracting Process

Last year, after the establishment of the illegal organization in the puppet state, which took control of the section of the Beining Railway from Shenyang to Shanhaiguan and established the Fengshan Railway Bureau, traffic between inside and outside the pass was blocked. Later, due to the needs of the situation, both China and Japan, in order to maintain traffic, after several consultations, decided that a third party should come forward to contract the through train service while avoiding recognition of the puppet organization in principle. At that time, the Chinese government greatly favored the China Travel Service to come forward to handle it. After repeated urging by the Ministry of Railways, the company reluctantly agreed to participate and organized the Oriental Travel Agency to undertake the arduous task. It was ordered to start contracting the Peiping-Shenyang through train service from July 1st, but because this matter was of great importance, it was unwilling to be permanently responsible and agreed with the Ministry of Railways to conduct a pilot operation for six months, which would end immediately. By the end of last December, the contracting matter had expired. The company's board of directors reported to the Ministry of Railways, requesting that it stop participating and handle the termination in accordance with the agreement. Yesterday, the company received an official letter from the Ministry of Railways approving the record and termination. According to Mr. Chen Xiangtao, manager of the company, to a reporter from Dagongbao, our company's participation in the contracting of the through train service has come to an end. After the termination of the Oriental Travel Agency, the problem of through train service between Peiping and Shenyang will be handled by the government. It is not yet known whether another organization will be formed. Our company has been operating the through train service for six months and is fortunate to have done so without any faults to the people, he said.

Notice of Termination

The Shanghai China Travel Service headquarters issued a notice of termination yesterday, which stated: "Notice: Our company was ordered to participate in the organization of the Oriental Travel Agency from July 1st last year, and it was agreed to conduct a pilot operation for six months, which expired at the end of last year. We reported to the Ministry of Railways, stating that we would stop participating in accordance with the agreement from January 1st this year and requested a record to be terminated. We have now received the Ministry of Railways' official letter No. 2691, approving the record, etc. Our company has completely terminated the case of participating in the Oriental Travel Agency. We hereby declare this, and we hope you will take note."

Nanjing Road Citizens' Association Opposes Telephone Rate Increase

The Shanghai Telephone Company has recently requested the Shanghai Municipal Council to approve an increase in user telephone rates. All sectors of society believe that the market is sluggish to the extreme and that it is unbearable to drain the pond to catch the fish, so they unanimously expressed their opposition. Yesterday, the Nanjing Road Citizens' Association specially convened a meeting for this matter. It was unanimously resolved to send letters to the Shanghai Citizens' General Association, the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, and the Municipal Chamber of Commerce to reiterate the previous resolution and demand that they make persistent efforts to protest the telephone rate increase to the Shanghai Municipal Council. They also discussed the Revival Movement and resolved to reduce rents and lower the prices of electricity and tap water to alleviate the people's difficulties. These suggestions were included in the letters to the above-mentioned groups in order to promote the realization of the Revival Movement, it is said.

Ma Siliang, Special Military Commissioner for Sichuan, Returned to China Yesterday

Mr. Ma Talks About the Tense Situation in Europe

National News Agency reports: Mr. Ma Siliang, the special commissioner sent by the Sichuan Provincial Government to Europe to study military affairs, has recently returned from his study in Europe. A reporter from the National News Agency made a special trip to his lodging yesterday to interview him and received a detailed account. Mr. Ma said that he was ordered by the provincial government to go to Europe to study military affairs and set off last April, arriving successively in England, France, Germany, Switzerland, Czech Republic, Austria, Italy, and other seven countries, for a total of nine months. On the eve of the Second World War, all countries were making every effort to strengthen their national defense capabilities as a prerequisite, paying attention to the national defense industry and the secrecy of manufacturing weapons. The political emphasis of various countries and the deep-rooted national concept of the people were truly moving to him. As he returns to his homeland, he has infinite expectations for his motherland. In the nine months apart, the motherland has made some progress, such as the gradual realization of unity and the gradual completion of construction projects. Mr. Ma will stay in Shanghai for a short time and then return to Sichuan to report, he said.

Completion of the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou Line of the Nine-Province Telephone Network

Currently Measuring the Shanghai-Hankou and Other Four Lines

800,000 Yuan in Funding Has Been Allocated by the State

Huadong News Agency reports: The long-distance telephone network of the nine provinces of Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Henan, Shandong, Hubei, Hunan, and Hebei, which is being constructed by the Ministry of Communications, has completed the surveying and erection of poles for the Beijing-Shanghai-Hangzhou lines. The surveying of the Shanghai-Hankou, Beijing-Tianjin, Pinghan, and Longhai lines is currently underway. The Ministry of Communications sent Chen Gengfa, Chief of Engineering for the Shanghai-Hankou Line, to Hankou to survey the route between Hankou and Qiupu, and Li Guohua, Chief of Engineering for the Qingpu Line, to survey the route between Qiupu and Nanjing. Both men have now completed their route surveying work and are currently carrying out measurement work. Once the measurement is completed, pole erection and wire laying will begin. It is said that the Beijing-Tianjin line will be erected from Tianjin in the north, and the Tianjin-Jinan section and the Qiupu-Nanjing section will be completed first. The Jinan-Xuzhou-Bengbu-Beijing sections are expected to be surveyed and construction will begin this year. The Ministry of Communications has specially sent Liu Songchou, a long-distance telephone administrator, to Xuzhou to inspect the telephone between Xuzhou and Haizhou and to visit Lianyungang for inspection. According to both men to the Huadong News Agency reporter, the Ministry of Communications will set up a general line station at the Tianjin-Longhai junction of the long-distance telephone in Xuzhou. As for the total cost, it has been approved by the Executive Yuan to use the state's second reserve fund, totaling 800,000 yuan. The entire completion of the call period must be realized after two years, it is said.

Will Fly to Xinjiang Soon to Meet Sheng

Huadong News Agency reports: Li Jingcong, General Manager of the Eurasia Aviation Corporation, returned to Shanghai from Nanjing yesterday. A reporter from the Huadong News Agency made a special trip to the company to interview him. Secretary Zha Zhenhu received the reporter in his place. The details are recorded as follows:

Li Sheng's Telegram

According to Secretary Zha, Manager Li arrived in Shanghai this morning (yesterday). The report that Manager Li went to Xinjiang to plan the restoration of the Shanghai-Xinjiang air route is a misrepresentation. As for the restoration of the Shanghai-Xinjiang air route, this matter is also very complicated. At the end of last year, Sheng Shicai, the governor of Xinjiang Province, sent a telegram to Manager Li, stating that Xinjiang Province planned to independently manage the Hami-Tacheng section of the air route and inquired about the company's opinion. After receiving the telegram, Li considered the matter to be serious and did not reply without authorization. He then forwarded it to Zhu Jiahua, Minister of Communications, to ask for instructions. Subsequently, the Ministry of Communications approved him to temporarily operate on his own. Manager Li also telegraphed the opinion of the Ministry of Communications to Governor Sheng, asking him to prepare as soon as possible.

Flying to Xinjiang Soon

Secretary Zha continued, "At the beginning of this month, Governor Sheng sent another telegram, requesting the company to extend the air route to Hami by the end of this month so that the aircraft independently prepared by Xinjiang Province can connect and fly to Tacheng, and instructed to quickly set up a Hami office." After reading the telegram, Li considered the procedures for this matter to be very important and did not agree hastily. He then telegraphed Sheng in Xinjiang to inquire about the method of transportation and all the procedures. A reply is expected within days. Once it arrives, Manager Li will fly to Xinjiang in person to negotiate, he said.

Hydrographic Bureau Assists in Surveying and Dredging the Shentan, Starting in Early April

The Tai Dredger Will Arrive in Shanghai at the End of Next Month

The Ship's Crew Is Stipulated to Be 70 People

The Location of the Shoal Belongs to Tongsha and Guansha

Datong News Agency reports: The General Dredging Bureau ordered the world's largest dredger from the Schichau Shipyard in Germany, which set sail to China on the 8th of this month, with an estimated voyage of two months, as has been reported in the newspapers. A Datong News Agency reporter made a special trip to visit Dr. Chadley, Chief Engineer of the Bureau, yesterday morning and learned that the ship is expected to arrive in Shanghai by the end of next month, and that the surveying of the Shentan has already begun. The details are recorded as follows:

Shoal Names Tongsha and Guansha

Regarding the dredging of the Shentan outside the Wusongkou, due to the scale of the project, the Hydrographic Bureau of the Ministry of the Navy is providing assistance with surveying. The survey has now been completed. The location of the shoal is actually southeast of the Shentan, and its place names are Tongsha and Guansha, which is the center of the Yangtze River estuary, 20 English miles from the mouth of the Yangtze River and 30 English miles from the Wusongkou. After completing the survey, the Hydrographic Bureau has drawn and printed detailed maps for the Dredging Bureau to refer to when the dredging project begins.

Crew Set at 70 People

Regarding the Havas dispatch about the departure of the large dredger to China, which was reported in the newspapers yesterday morning, Mr. Zha said that there were some discrepancies. Regarding the crew of the ship, after arriving in Shanghai, the four or five crew members sent by the Schichau Shipyard are still planning to be retained as skilled workers, not all Chinese workers. However, in addition to these four or five people, the quota for crew members is stipulated to be 70 people, and the remaining 60 or so people will be all Chinese, he said. The amount of sand, stone, and mud that can be excavated daily is approximately 20,000 cubic meters, not 25,000 cubic meters. The above-mentioned dredging will start in early April.

The large dredger is expected to arrive in Shanghai by the end of next month, so the dredging project of Tongsha and Guansha outside the Wusongkou will likely begin in early April. According to Mr. Zha's research, the mud quality there is no different from the mud quality in the Huangpu River, except that it is slightly slippery. The stipulated dredging length is 20 English miles, and a width of only 1,000 feet is sufficient. It was previously said that there were also plans to widen it to 20 English miles, but that was a reporter's misunderstanding, he said.

Ma Xiaochun, Standing Committee Member of the Kunming Chamber of Commerce, Discusses Yunnan's Commercial Situation

Foreign Goods Flood the Market, Urgent Need to Promote Domestic Products

Scheduled to Depart for Yunnan on the 20th to Participate in the National Exhibition

According to the Shen Shi News Agency, Mr. Ma Xiaochun, Standing Committee Member of the Kunming Chamber of Commerce in Yunnan Province, came to Shanghai to arrange everything for the preparation of the Yunnan National Exhibition and is scheduled to return to Yunnan on the 20th of this month to attend the opening ceremony of the National Exhibition. The Shen Shi News Agency reporter visited Mr. Ma at his residence yesterday and was informed of the following:

Mission to Shanghai

According to Mr. Ma, Yunnan Province is remote due to inconvenient transportation, and its commerce has been little developed as a result, leading to a flood of foreign goods in the market. Before the September 18th Incident, Japanese goods almost dominated the Yunnan market. After that, due to the boycott movement, Japanese goods decreased, but because of Kunming's proximity to Annam (Vietnam), French goods replaced Japanese goods. This phenomenon is very worrying. The Department of Industry has therefore taken measures to hold national product exhibitions and establish national product companies in order to develop the national product market and recover lost profits. As for the global economic recession, because Yunnan is remote, the impact on commerce has been minimal.

Scheduled Return to Yunnan

Yunnan's industry is still in the extremely nascent stage of handicrafts, barely enough for self-sufficiency. In terms of education, the province has one university, more than ten middle schools, and seventy or eighty elementary schools, but popular education is very developed, which is a special and good phenomenon. My visit here is to arrange for the Yunnan National Products Exhibition and the collection of goods for the National Products Company. Methods have been established with the China National Products Production and Sales Cooperation Association. The goods for participation have already been shipped and have now arrived in Kunming. I am scheduled to leave Shanghai on the 20th of this month in order to attend the opening ceremony of the exhibition.

The Social Affairs Bureau Decides to Thoroughly Investigate the Yih Ho Factory Strike

Workers Petitioned the Social Affairs Bureau Yesterday Morning

The Yih Ho Cotton Mill's new factory in Yangtzepoo, Shanghai, has over 1,500 workers. Recently, because the factory foremen deducted wages, over 700 workers hired several trucks yesterday morning at 9:30 AM and went to the city center to petition the Social Affairs Bureau. When passing the City Police Branch in the city center, the police, due to the large number of people, stopped them and ordered them to elect representatives. The workers elected five representatives, prepared a document, and went to the Social Affairs Bureau, where they were received by Mr. Wang Xianqing, Director of the Mediation Division, who promised to investigate and handle the matter immediately. The five representatives returned and told all the workers that they were satisfied. The Social Affairs Bureau scheduled to send personnel to conduct a thorough investigation yesterday afternoon at 1:00 PM, together with the Municipal Party Department, in order to carry out mediation.

The Cigarette Industry Association Submits Proposals for Relief of the Cigarette Industry

Submitted to the Tax Office Yesterday for Forwarding to the Ministry of Finance for Adoption

The Shanghai Chinese Cigarette Factory Industry Association, because the cigarette industry in our country is declining day by day, yesterday submitted a proposal to the Tax Office for forwarding to the Ministry of Finance, requesting its adoption and implementation. The original text is as follows: We hereby report that the cigarette industry, from October 1, 1930, to the end of March 1931, within the scope of the unified tax area, the average monthly sales of machine-made cigarettes was 102,408 cases (50,000 cigarettes per case). Since the increase in the cigarette tax rate in January 1932, the monthly average number, up to the end of December 1933, has dropped to 90,450 cases (50,000 cigarettes per case). From December 5, 1933, to October 1934, the tax rate was increased again, and the number dropped to 78,358 cases (50,000 cigarettes per case). The above-mentioned decline is partly due to the business environment, such as the economic recession and the decline in the value of copper coins, which have reduced the purchasing power of the general public. However, these are only indirect reasons. The main points of its non-connection are as follows: (1) The tax rate on machine-made cigarettes is too far from the tax rate on hand-made cigarettes. (2) The development of hand-made cigarette manufacturing and sales within the tax zone. (3) The reason for the development of hand-made cigarettes is that the government collects taxes on hand-made cigarettes regardless of grade, averaging 10 yuan per 50,000 cigarettes. This tax rate is only one-eighth of the lowest tax rate for machine-made cigarettes. The evasion of taxes cannot be stopped, and the sales of illicit cigarettes are increasing day by day. Machine-made cigarettes are the biggest reason for the decline in business. When the regulations restricting hand-made cigarettes were promulgated in 1930, the business of hand-made cigarettes was limited to Bengbu in Anhui and Xuzhou in Henan, small towns in remote areas. But now, Anhui, Henan, Shandong, Hebei, Jiangxi, and other provinces and towns are all over the place. According to rough calculations, the average daily sales of hand-made cigarettes is about 20,000 cases (50,000 cigarettes per case). In terms of tax revenue, machine-made cigarette merchants have suffered huge losses due to the development of hand-made cigarettes, and the tax revenue collected by the government from hand-made cigarettes is actually equal to zero. From our experience, the current cigarette tax rate regulations can indeed promote the development of hand-made cigarette business. Not only that, hand-made cigarettes often counterfeit the registered trademarks of machine-made cigarettes, and this has become even more serious recently. The current laws on the punishment of counterfeiting trademarks and the protection of registered trademarks are not sufficient to prohibit such behavior in practice. In order to relieve the machine-made cigarette business and maintain the government's tax revenue, we respectfully submit the following suggestions as far as our humble opinions can reach: (1) Increase the tax rate on hand-made cigarettes to be equal to the lowest tax rate for machine-made cigarettes, or issue a separate law that prohibits the manufacture of cigarettes unless by legally registered manufacturers, and must be strictly enforced, and counterfeit trademarks should be punished. Special attention should be paid to the above-mentioned hand-made cigarette areas. (2) Formulate strict implementation measures for the regulations restricting the import of cigarette paper, so that all illegally tax-evaded cigarettes cannot be manufactured. (3) Strictly supervise the collection agencies for the unified tobacco leaf tax to prevent tax-evading tobacco leaves from flooding everywhere and being used by hand-made cigarette manufacturers. (4) Expand the powers of the Cigarette Smuggling Suppression Committee so that it can fully implement smuggling suppression. For example, comparing the tobacco leaf tax in the Zhengzhou area of Henan in 1934 with that of 1933, it has increased by 30%. The above points and their relief methods are respectfully requested to be reviewed by your office and forwarded to the Ministry of Finance for adoption and implementation, so as to ease business difficulties and increase tax revenue. Respectfully, to the Tax Office of the Ministry of Finance.

Kong Wu and Others Telegraph to Aediff to Repair Water Conservancy

Kong Xiangxi, Chairman of the Drought Relief Association, and others, telegraphed to Mr. Aediff, Chairman of the China Foreign Famine Relief Committee, yesterday, saying: "To Mr. Aediff, China Foreign Famine Relief Committee, Hu Cai Chang Hutong, Peiping, knowing well: This association believes that frequent natural disasters in recent years are actually due to the disrepair of water conservancy. We now intend to carry out work relief to remedy this. After investigation, the areas most severely affected in recent years are Changyuan, Puyang, and Dongming counties. We plan to start with these three counties. However, we feel that there is a lack of personnel familiar with engineering. We have long admired your committee's outstanding achievements in handling work relief in various provinces over the years. After discussing with Mr. Baker, a consultant to the association, we telegraphed you, first requesting you to send personnel to Changyuan to investigate and find out the details of the disaster suffered by the county, and how to repair the rivers and benefits. Please show us a detailed plan. We hope you will agree. We are extremely grateful. More details will be provided in a letter. Kong Xiangxi, Xu Shiying, Wang Zhengting, Wang Yiting, Wu Tiecheng, kowtow."

The Counterfeit Franc Case Awaits Sentencing

Chen Jiannan, a native of Wenzhou, 47 years old, had been running a restaurant in Brazil for 23 years. He returned to his hometown last April. At the end of December, he arrived in Shanghai by ship and stayed in room 30 at the Yong'an Hotel at 24 Dongyouheng Road, planning to go to Brazil again. He was discovered by Chinese detective Zhu Shanghe of the Huishan Police Station to be in possession of counterfeit currency. On January 9, at 5:00 PM, he reported to the head detective and secretly went with a Western detective to arrest Chen. They found 920 five-franc coins and 516 ten-franc coins in his luggage, placed flat in a white cloth long vest, sewn tightly with thread, worn from the top, and covered with an overcoat, so no one knew. They also found two counterfeit Chinese currency yuan, four counterfeit dimes, and 51 genuine five-yuan Shanghai banknotes in his pockets and took them all to the police station. He confessed to the First Special District Court that he had bought the francs and counterfeit silver dimes from a Mr. Someone he did not know on the ship when he came to Shanghai, spending 100 yuan, to take to Brazil for use, and that he did not know they were counterfeit, etc. He was instructed to reschedule the hearing and have experts authenticate the francs. The defendant was remanded in custody. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan opened the Third Criminal Court for a hearing. Mr. Li Zhishan, a lawyer for the Shanghai Municipal Council, stated that the francs had been authenticated by experts from a French bank as completely counterfeit. Photographs of the genuine and counterfeit currencies were taken, clearly distinguishing them. He presented a large album of these photos for inspection. When questioned, the defendant insisted that the francs and counterfeit silver dimes belonged to Mr. Someone on the ship and that he had been deceived. The rest of his testimony was evasive. He asked for leniency. Judge Wu ordered that he remain in custody and scheduled a sentencing date.

Three Robbers Attempted to Rob Without Success

The Case was Cracked at the Greater China Hotel

Currently, the police station has not yet investigated the case due to time constraints, and the seized handguns must be sent to the Shanghai Municipal Council's Armory for inspection. An Autopsy of the Old Woman Found in the Opium Den Fire on Xiamen Road

Later, the detectives learned that the old woman's name was Ye Ai, 69 years old, a native of Sancaitang, Pudong. She had no children and was from a poor family. She usually carried a basket and sold chicken and duck eggs along the streets of Shanghai every day. She happened to be passing by the facility that day when she was crushed to death. The detectives took the body to the autopsy station on Faelun Road. Tang then ordered an examination, which confirmed that the deceased, Ye Ai, was female and had been crushed to death by the collapsed building. The body was released to Liu Ye, the daughter of the deceased, who signed a receipt for its return for burial.

Brave Detectives Rescue Kidnapped Victim Wang Boying

One Bandit Killed, Four Male and Three Female Bandits Captured Alive

Rescued from Rongfuli, Western Aihuiamus Road

Victim Wounded by Stray Bullet, Immediately Sent to Guangci Hospital

Wang Boying (38 years old), a director of the Great Eastern Book Company from Shaoxing, Zhejiang, was kidnapped on the morning of the 10th of this month at 0:10 AM when he was returning from an outing in his private car to his residence at No. 7 Changfengli, Tongfu Road. When the car reached the alley entrance, three kidnappers, two men and one woman, suddenly kidnapped him. At the same time, they drove the chauffeur, Feng Futang, near the Great World and abandoned him there, hiding the victim without a trace. Wang's car was discovered in the French Concession on Guofumin Road in the afternoon. Details have been recorded in this newspaper. Since the case occurred, the police authorities of both the Chinese and Foreign concessions in this port have made every effort to investigate. Miraculously, only four days later, the case was completely solved. When the detectives stormed the bandits' den, the bandits opened fire to resist arrest. One bandit was killed on the spot by the detectives, and a total of four male and three female bandits were captured alive. The kidnapped victim, Wang Boying, was wounded in the left arm by a stray bullet but was not seriously injured. The details are recorded below:

A Female Guest at the Dafa Hotel

Around midnight the day before yesterday, a female guest, dressed fashionably and about 20 years old, suddenly came to the Dafa Hotel on Zhengjia Muqiao Street in the French Concession. She registered under the name He Xiuying, a local, and booked room 201 on the second floor of the hotel. At first, there was nothing unusual. Yesterday morning, two men came to the room and closed the door for a secret conversation with the female guest. The waiters and others did not pay much attention.

Chinese and Western Detectives Search for Kidnappers

Yesterday, at around 11:00 AM, the Chengdu Road Police Station in the Public Concession suddenly received a telephone tip that the kidnappers of Wang Boying were in room 201 of the Dafa Hotel. The station immediately ordered Chinese and Western detectives to join forces with detectives from the French Police Station and went to the address to arrest the woman, He Xiuying, and two young men. From their confession, they learned that there were other accomplices in room 308 of the Dazhong Hotel (the old site of the Hong Kong Hotel) across the street. The detectives then went to the Dazhong Hotel and arrested another male bandit, Cai Bingyun, and a female bandit.

He Xiuying Confesses the Location of the Victim

After capturing all the bandits, they were all taken to the Lujiiawan Police Station and interrogated rigorously. The female bandit He Xiuying confessed that the kidnapped victim Wang Boying was being held in the headquarters at No. 14 Rongfuli, Western Aihuiamus Road, in the French Concession. Based on her confession, the police chief led the female bandit to the destination at 12:20 PM, accompanied by Wan Langdeng, the first chief of the police department, and Jin Jiulin, the chief inspector, Zheng Tanmu, Zhou Bingcheng, Bao Tan, Liu Dianlong, and others bravely stormed into the bandits' den.

Detectives and Bandits Fought Like Linked Pearls

When the detectives reached their destination, there were three male and female bandits guarding the victim in the bandits' den. They were prepared and opened fire as the detectives rushed in, firing four or five shots in total. All shots missed. At this time, the detectives also opened fire in retaliation. Both sides were like confronting a major enemy, and the gunfire was as dense as linked pearls. The stalemate lasted for more than ten minutes.

One Bandit Killed, Victim Rescued

As a result, a male bandit wearing a grey woolen student uniform was shot three times in the chest and hand and fell to the ground dead. The kidnapped victim, Zhu Boying, was also hit in the arm by a stray bullet. The detectives rescued him from danger, and the remaining two male and female bandits surrendered without resistance and were taken back to the police station. After a brief interrogation by the police chief and registration, they were handed over to Chinese and Western detectives from Chengdu Road to be brought back for interrogation and handling.

Police Station Must Continue to Pursue Remaining Accomplices

The injured Wang Boying was immediately escorted to Guangci Hospital on Avenue Dubail for treatment. It is heard that he is not in serious condition. At the same time, the police chief sent Bao Tan Zhang Chunsheng to Rongfuli to take the body of the killed bandit to the autopsy station. According to the arrested bandits, the dead bandit's name was Yao Muqing, 25 years old, from Wuxi. The case will be reported to the court for inspection today. The police station is continuing to investigate the remaining accomplices.
